# mapping
# ng/ñ -> r
# oe/ö -> j
# eo/ö -> j
# yu/ü -> v
# aa/ā -> r
# gw/ģ -> x
# kw/ķ -> q
# j/y  -> y

# keyboard layout
# ķ w/oi e    ā     t/öi ö    u    i    ñ/o  p
# a s/ai d/ei f/āi  g/ui h/iu y/ou k/āu l/au
# z ģ    c    ü     b    n    m
